      "source": [
        "def load_description(text):\n",
        "\tmapping = dict()\n",
        "\tfor line in text.split(\"\\n\"):\n",
        "\t\ttoken = line.split(\",\")\n",
        "\t\tif len(line) < 2:\n",
        "\t\t\tcontinue\n",
        "\t\timg_id = token[0].split('.')[0]\n",
        "\t\timg_des = token[1]\n",
        "\t\tif img_id not in mapping:\n",
        "\t\t\tmapping[img_id] = list()\n",
        "\t\tmapping[img_id].append(img_des)\n",
        "\treturn mapping\n"
      ]
    },

      "source": [
        "import string\n",
        "\n",
        "def clean_description(desc):\n",
        "\tfor key, des_list in desc.items():\n",
        "\t\tfor i in range(len(des_list)):\n",
        "\t\t\tcaption = des_list[i]\n",
        "\t\t\tcaption = [ch for ch in caption if ch not in string.punctuation]\n",
        "\t\t\tcaption = ''.join(caption)\n",
        "\t\t\tcaption = caption.split(' ')\n",
        "\t\t\tcaption = [word.lower() for word in caption if len(word)>1 and word.isalpha()]\n",
        "\t\t\tcaption = ' '.join(caption)\n",
        "\t\t\tdes_list[i] = caption\n",
        "\n",
        "clean_description(descriptions)\n",
        "descriptions['1000268201_693b08cb0e']"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "execution_count": null,
      "metadata": {
        "id": "mTuazAOqRABy"
      },
      "outputs": [],
      "source": [
        "def to_vocab(desc):\n",
        "\twords = set()\n",
        "\tfor key in desc.keys():\n",
        "\t\tfor line in desc[key]:\n",
        "\t\t\twords.update(line.split())\n",
        "\treturn words\n",
        "vocab = to_vocab(descriptions)\n"
      ]
    },

      "source": [
        "# Get all image IDs from descriptions\n",
        "all_img_ids = list(descriptions.keys())\n",
        "\n",
        "# Shuffle the list of image IDs\n",
        "random.shuffle(all_img_ids)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Define split ratio for training and testing sets\n",
        "split_ratio = 0.5  # 80% training, 20% testing\n",
        "\n",
        "# Calculate the split index\n",
        "split_index = int(len(all_img_ids) * split_ratio)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Split into training and testing sets\n",
        "train_img_ids = all_img_ids[:split_index]\n",
        "test_img_ids = all_img_ids[split_index:]\n",
        "\n",
        "# Paths for output train and test image files\n",
        "train_images_file = '/content/drive/MyDrive/data/Flickr_8k.trainImages.txt'\n",
        "test_images_file = '/content/drive/MyDrive/data/Flickr_8k.testImages.txt'\n",
        "\n",
        "# Write the train image IDs to the train images file\n",
        "with open(train_images_file, 'w') as file:\n",
        "    for img_id in train_img_ids:\n",
        "        file.write(f\"{img_id}.jpg\\n\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# Write the test image IDs to the test images file\n",
        "with open(test_images_file, 'w') as file:\n",
        "    for img_id in test_img_ids:\n",
        "        file.write(f\"{img_id}.jpg\\n\")\n"
      ]
    },

        "id": "N9SA1X8Eb14Y"

      "outputs": [],
      "source": [
        "# Function to save descriptions\n",
        "def save_descriptions(descriptions, image_ids, filename):\n",
        "    with open(filename, 'w') as file:\n",
        "        for img_id in image_ids:\n",
        "            for desc in descriptions[img_id]:\n",
        "                file.write(f\"{img_id}\\t{desc}\\n\")\n",
        "\n",
        "train_descriptions_file = '/content/drive/MyDrive/data/Flickr_8k.trainDescriptions.txt'\n",
        "save_descriptions(descriptions, train_img_ids, train_descriptions_file)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Save testing descriptions\n",
        "test_descriptions_file = '/content/drive/MyDrive/data/Flickr_8k.testDescriptions.txt'\n",
        "save_descriptions(descriptions, test_img_ids, test_descriptions_file)\n"
      ]
    },

        "def load_clean_descriptions(des, dataset):\n",
        "\tdataset_des = dict()\n",
        "\tfor key, des_list in des.items():\n",
        "\t\tif key+'.jpg' in dataset:\n",
        "\t\t\tif key not in dataset_des:\n",
        "\t\t\t\tdataset_des[key] = list()\n",
        "\t\t\tfor line in des_list:\n",
        "\t\t\t\tdesc = 'startseq ' + line + ' endseq'\n",
        "\t\t\t\tdataset_des[key].append(desc)\n",
        "\treturn dataset_des\n",
        "\n",
        "train_descriptions = load_clean_descriptions(descriptions, train_images)\n",
        "print(train_descriptions['1000268201_693b08cb0e'])\n"

        "from keras.preprocessing.image import load_img, img_to_array\n",
        "def preprocess_img(img_path):\n",
        "\t# inception v3 excepts img in 299 * 299 * 3\n",
        "\timg = load_img(img_path, target_size = (299, 299))\n",
        "\tx = img_to_array(img)\n",
        "\t# Add one more dimension\n",
        "\tx = np.expand_dims(x, axis = 0)\n",
        "\tx = preprocess_input(x)\n",
        "\treturn x\n",
        "\n",
        "def encode(image):\n",
        "\timage = preprocess_img(image)\n",
        "\tvec = model.predict(image)\n",
        "\tvec = np.reshape(vec, (vec.shape[1]))\n",
        "\treturn vec\n",
        "\n",
        "base_model = InceptionV3(weights = 'imagenet')\n",
        "model = Model(base_model.input, base_model.layers[-2].output)\n",
        "# run the encode function on all train images and store the feature vectors in a list\n",
        "encoding_train = {}\n",
        "for img in train_img:\n",
        "\tencoding_train[img[len(images):]] = encode(img)\n"

        "# list of all training captions\n",
        "all_train_captions = []\n",
        "for key, val in train_descriptions.items():\n",
        "\tfor caption in val:\n",
        "\t\tall_train_captions.append(caption)\n",
        "\n",
        "# consider only words which occur atleast 10 times\n",
        "vocabulary = vocab\n",
        "threshold = 10 # you can change this value according to your need\n",
        "word_counts = {}\n",
        "for cap in all_train_captions:\n",
        "\tfor word in cap.split(' '):\n",
        "\t\tword_counts[word] = word_counts.get(word, 0) + 1\n",
        "\n",
        "vocab = [word for word in word_counts if word_counts[word] >= threshold]\n",
        "\n",
        "# word mapping to integers\n",
        "ixtoword = {}\n",
        "wordtoix = {}\n",
        "\n",
        "ix = 1\n",
        "for word in vocab:\n",
        "\twordtoix[word] = ix\n",
        "\tixtoword[ix] = word\n",
        "\tix += 1\n",
        "\n",
        "# find the maximum length of a description in a dataset\n",
        "max_length = max(len(des.split()) for des in all_train_captions)\n",
        "max_length\n"

        "for key, des_list in train_descriptions.items():\n",

        "\t\tseq = [wordtoix[word] for word in cap.split(' ') if word in wordtoix]\n",
        "\t\tfor i in range(1, len(seq)):\n",
        "\t\t\tin_seq, out_seq = seq[:i], seq[i]\n",
        "\t\t\tin_seq = pad_sequences([in_seq], maxlen = max_length)[0]\n",
        "\t\t\tout_seq = to_categorical([out_seq], num_classes = vocab_size)[0]\n",
        "\t\t\t# store\n",

        "golve_path ='/content/drive/MyDrive/data/glove.6B.200d.txt'\n",

        "for line in glove.split(\"\\n\"):\n",
        "\tvalues = line.split(\" \")\n",
        "\tword = values[0]\n",
        "\tindices = np.asarray(values[1: ], dtype = 'float32')\n",
        "\tembeddings_index[word] = indices\n",

        "# define the model\n",
        "ip1 = Input(shape = (2048, ))\n",
        "fe1 = Dropout(0.2)(ip1)\n",
        "fe2 = Dense(256, activation = 'relu')(fe1)\n",
        "ip2 = Input(shape = (max_length, ))\n",
        "se1 = Embedding(vocab_size, emb_dim, mask_zero = True)(ip2)\n",
        "se2 = Dropout(0.2)(se1)\n",
        "se3 = LSTM(256)(se2)\n",
        "decoder1 = add([fe2, se3])\n",
        "decoder2 = Dense(256, activation = 'relu')(decoder1)\n",
        "outputs = Dense(vocab_size, activation = 'softmax')(decoder2)\n",
        "model = Model(inputs = [ip1, ip2], outputs = outputs)\n"
      ]

        "def encode(image_path, model):\n",
        "    # Preprocess the image\n",
        "    image = preprocess_img(image_path)\n",
        "    # Generate the feature vector for the image\n",
        "    feature_vector = model.predict(image)\n",
        "    # Reshape the vector to match the required input shape\n",
        "    feature_vector = np.reshape(feature_vector, (feature_vector.shape[1]))\n",
        "    return feature_vector\n",
        "\n",
        "# Assuming you have already initialized your base model for encoding\n",
        "base_model = InceptionV3(weights='imagenet')\n",
        "encoding_model = Model(base_model.input, base_model.layers[-2].output)\n"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "ByqVug4wRxIH"
      },
      "execution_count": null,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "def greedy_search(encoded_img):\n",
        "    # Starting token\n",
        "    start = 'startseq'\n",
        "\n",
        "    for i in range(max_length):\n",
        "        # Convert start sequence to index sequence\n",
        "        seq = [wordtoix[word] for word in start.split() if word in wordtoix]\n",
        "        # Pad sequence to max_length\n",
        "        seq = pad_sequences([seq], maxlen=max_length)\n",
        "        # Predict the next word\n",
        "        yhat = model.predict([encoded_img, seq], verbose=0)\n",
        "        # Get the word with max probability\n",
        "        yhat = np.argmax(yhat)\n",
        "        # Map integer to word\n",
        "        word = ixtoword[yhat]\n",
        "        # Append word to the sequence\n",
        "        start += ' ' + word\n",
        "        # If end sequence token is predicted, stop\n",
        "        if word == 'endseq':\n",
        "            break\n",
        "\n",
        "    # Clean the generated sequence\n",
        "    final_caption = start.split()\n",
        "    final_caption = final_caption[1:-1]  # Remove startseq and endseq\n",
        "    final_caption = ' '.join(final_caption)\n",
        "\n",
        "    return final_caption\n"
      ],
      "metadata": {
        "id": "gweyRfo9VEJK"
      },
      "execution_count": null,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "source": [
        "\n",
        "from google.colab.patches import cv2_imshow\n",
        "# Path to a new image\n",
        "new_image_path = '/content/Screenshot 2024-07-28 232204.png'\n",
        "\n",
        "# Encode the image\n",
        "encoded_img = encode(new_image_path, encoding_model)\n",
        "\n",
        "# Reshape the encoded image to match the model input\n",
        "encoded_img = np.reshape(encoded_img, (1, 2048))\n",
        "\n",
        "# Generate a caption using the greedy search\n",
        "caption = greedy_search(encoded_img)\n",
        "print(\"Generated Caption:\", caption)\n",
